This works when `self.query.selected is None` (the normal case), where the select list is built as extras followed by model columns followed by annotations. However, when `self.query.selected is not None`, the column positions shift because selected fields are inserted first, breaking the index calculation.\n\nWith `values_list(Concat(...), \"born\")`, the annotation gets placed before the model column in the selected dict, so the code incorrectly assumes the model column is at position 0 when it's actually the annotation, causing an AttributeError when trying to access the model.\n\nThe fix needs to handle the `else` branch of `get_select()` when `self.query.selected is not None` by recalculating the actual positions of model columns instead of relying on the hardcoded offset assumption.\n\n```\n\npython\nelse:\n    col_select_fields = []\n    for alias, expression in self.query.selected.items():\n        # Reference to an annotation.\n        if isinstance(expression, str):\n            expression = self.query.annotations[expression]\n        # Reference to a column.\n        elif isinstance(expression, int):\n            col_select_fields.append(len(selected))  # track actual position\n            expression = cols[expression]\n        # ColPairs cannot be aliased.\n        if isinstance(expression, ColPairs):\n            alias = None\n        selected.append((alias, expression))\n    if klass_info is not None:\n        klass_info[\"select_fields\"] = col_select_fields\n```\n\nBuilding the fix...\n\nI'm realizing there's another issue with `_get_parent_klass_info()` — it assumes `select_index` always points to a `Col` expression and tries to access `.target.model` directly, which will fail if it's an annotation. This assumption is correct only when `self.query.selected is None` (the non-values() case), because then the `selected` list is constructed in a fixed order: extras → model cols → annotations.\n\n  When `values_list()` or `values()` is used with annotation expressions, `self.query.selected is not None` and iteration order over `self.query.selected.items()` determines column positions. `set_values()` inserts annotation references before model column references if the user put expressions first (e.g. `values_list(Concat(...), \"born\")`). ColPairs cannot be aliased.\n                 if isinstance(expression, ColPairs):\n                     alias = None\n                 selected.append((alias, expression))\n+            if klass_info is not None:\n+                klass_info[\"select_fields\"] = col_select_fields\n```\n\nThis replaces the stale, order-assuming `select_fields` with the real positions of model-column expressions in the output `selected` list, making `get_select_for_update_of_arguments()` safe regardless of what order the user supplies fields and annotations to `values()`/`values_list()`.\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Step-by-step trace\n\n**User code:**\n```python\nPerson.objects.select_for_update(of=(\"self\",)).values_list(\n    Concat(Value(\"Dr. \"), F(\"name\")), \"born\"\n)\n```\n\n**1. `values_list()` in `django/db/models/query.py` (~line 1369)**\n\n`Concat(...)` has `resolve_expression`, so it is assigned the generated key `\"concat1\"` and stored in `expressions = {\"concat1\": Concat(...)}`. `_fields = [\"concat1\", \"born\"]`. `_values(\"concat1\", \"born\", concat1=Concat(...))` is called.\n\n**2. `_values()` (~line 1355)**\n\nCalls `clone.annotate(concat1=Concat(...))` (adds to `query.annotations` and `query.annotation_select`) then `query.set_values([\"concat1\", \"born\"])`.\n\n**3. `set_values()` in `django/db/models/sql/query.py` (~line 2492)**\n\nBecause annotations are non-empty, the shortcut is skipped. `default_cols = False`. Symptom observed in: `django/db/models/sql/compiler.py` — `_get_first_selected_col_from_model()` (~line 1440) and `_get_parent_klass_info()` (~line 1424) when they call `.target.model` on an annotation expression\n2. Called from: `django/db/models/sql/compiler.py` — `get_select_for_update_of_arguments()` (~line 1473)\n3. Bug triggered by: `django/db/models/sql/compiler.py` — `get_select()` (~line 262–267)\n4. Setup path: `django/db/models/query.py` — `values_list()` → `_values()` → `query.set_values()` in `django/db/models/sql/query.py`\n\n## Root Cause\n- **File**: `django/db/models/sql/compiler.py`\n- **Function**: `get_select()`\n- **Line**: ~262–267\n- **Explanation**: `get_select()` pre-computes `klass_info[\"select_fields\"]` as `range(len(extra_select), len(extra_select) + len(cols))`, which hard-codes the assumption that model field columns occupy sequential positions starting right after the extra-select entries in `self.select`. This assumption is correct only when `self.query.selected is None` (the non-values() case), because then the `selected` list is constructed in a fixed order: extras → model cols → annotations.\n\n  When `values_list()` or `values()` is used with annotation expressions, `self.query.selected is not None` and iteration order over `self.query.selected.items()` determines column positions. `set_values()` inserts annotation references before model column references if the user put expressions first (e.g. `values_list(Concat(...), \"born\")`). In that case `self.select[0]` is the `Concat` expression, not a model `Col` — but `klass_info[\"select_fields\"]` still says `[0]`, pointing to a model column that isn't there.\n\n  Later, `get_select_for_update_of_arguments()` → `_get_first_selected_col_from_model()` iterates `klass_info[\"select_fields\"]` and does `self.select[select_index][0].target.model`. Since `self.select[0][0]` is a `Concat` (or other annotation) expression — which has no `.target` attribute — this raises `AttributeError`.\n\n## Proposed Fix\n\nIn `get_select()`, when `self.query.selected is not None`, track the actual positions of model column entries (those where `expression` is an `int` — an index into `cols`) as the `selected` list is being built, and update `klass_info[\"select_fields\"]` accordingly:\n\n```diff\n--- a/django/db/models/sql/compiler.py\n+++ b/django/db/models/sql/compiler.py\n@@ -279,10 +279,16 @@ class SQLCompiler:\n         else:\n+            col_select_fields = []\n             for alias, expression in self.query.selected.items():\n                 # Reference to an annotation.\n                 if isinstance(expression, str):\n                     expression = self.query.annotations[expression]\n                 # Reference to a column.\n                 elif isinstance(expression, int):\n+                    col_select_fields.append(len(selected))\n                     expression = cols[expression]\n                 # ColPairs cannot be aliased.\n                 if isinstance(expression, ColPairs):\n                     alias = None\n                 selected.append((alias, expression))\n+            if klass_info is not None:\n+                klass_info[\"select_fields\"] = col_select_fields\n```\n\nThis replaces the stale, order-assuming `select_fields` with the real positions of model-column expressions in the output `selected` list, making `get_select_for_update_of_arguments()` safe regardless of what order the user supplies fields and annotations to `values()`/`values_list()`.\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Step-by-step trace\n\n**User code:**\n```python\nPerson.objects.select_for_update(of=(\"self\",)).values_list(\n    Concat(Value(\"Dr. \"), F(\"name\")), \"born\"\n)\n```\n\n**1. `values_list()` in `django/db/models/query.py` (~line 1369)**\n\n`Concat(...)` has `resolve_expression`, so it is assigned the generated key `\"concat1\"` and stored in `expressions = {\"concat1\": Concat(...)}`. `_fields = [\"concat1\", \"born\"]`. `_values(\"concat1\", \"born\", concat1=Concat(...))` is called.\n\n**2. `_values()` (~line 1355)**\n\nCalls `clone.annotate(concat1=Concat(...))` (adds to `query.annotations` and `query.annotation_select`) then `query.set_values([\"concat1\", \"born\"])`.\n\n**3. `set_values()` in `django/db/models/sql/query.py` (~line 2492)**\n\nBecause annotations are non-empty, the shortcut is skipped. `default_cols = False`. Iteration over `[\"concat1\", \"born\"]`:\n- `\"concat1\"` is in `annotation_select` → `selected[\"concat1\"] = \"concat1\"` (string reference)\n- `\"born\"` is a plain field → `field_names = [\"born\"]`, `selected[\"born\"] = 0` (integer index into cols)\n\n`self.selected = {\"concat1\": \"concat1\", \"born\": 0}`. Note: annotation entry comes **first**.\n\n**4. `get_select()` in `django/db/models/sql/compiler.py` (~line 230)**\n\n- `default_cols = False` → `cols = self.query.select` (resolved `Col` for `\"born\"`)\n- `len(cols) = 1`, `len(extra_select) = 0`\n- **Bug here**: `klass_info[\"select_fields\"] = list(range(0, 1)) = [0]` — assumes model col at position 0\n\nThen `self.query.selected is not None`, so the `else` branch runs:\n- `(\"concat1\", \"concat1\")` → str → `expression = Concat(...)` → appended at index 0\n- `(\"born\", 0)` → int → `expression = Col(\"born\")` → appended at index 1\n\nFinal `self.select = [(Concat(...), \"concat1\"), (Col(\"born\"), \"born\")]`\n\nBut `klass_info[\"select_fields\"] = [0]` still says the model column is at position 0, which is wrong.\n\n**5. `get_select_for_update_of_arguments()` (~line 1405)**\n\nFor `name = \"self\"` → `_get_first_selected_col_from_model(klass_info)`:\n```python\nfor select_index in [0]:  # select_fields\n    if self.select[0][0].target.model == concrete_model:  # Concat().target -> AttributeError!\n```\n\n`Concat` has no `.target` attribute → **`AttributeError: 'ConcatPair' object has no attribute 'target'`**\n\n### Why the fix is correct\n\nThe fix tracks each position where `isinstance(expression, int)` — i.e., a reference to a model column — as entries are appended to `selected`, then updates `klass_info[\"select_fields\"]` with these actual indices. After the fix, `select_fields = [1]` (the real position of `Col(\"born\")`), and `_get_first_selected_col_from_model()` correctly inspects `self.select[1][0] = Col(\"born\")`, which has `.target.model`, and proceeds without error.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":355,"cache_read_input_tokens":44551,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":355,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e4be08b3-2a7d-4eb3-ba8a-98ce4c5223e2","uuid":"a6a30f77-b64b-4c9c-a1ad-33d477adf7e0"}
